\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"webhook returned invalid response.patchType of %q\", patchType)\n80: \t\t\t\t}\n81: \t\t\t}\n82: \t\t} else {\n83: \t\t\t// Ensure a validating webhook doesn't return patch or patchType\n84: \t\t\tif len(r.Response.Patch) > 0 {\n85: \t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"validating webhook may not return response.patch\")\n86: \t\t\t}\n87: \t\t\tif r.Response.PatchType != nil {\n88: \t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"validating webhook may not return response.patchType\")\n89: \t\t\t}\n90: \t\t}\n91: \n92: \t\treturn &AdmissionResponse{\n93:       r.Response.Result,\n98: \t\t\tWarnings:         r.Response.Warnings,\n99: \t\t}, nil\n100: \n101: \tcase *admissionv1beta1.AdmissionReview:\n102: \t\tif r.Response == nil {\n103: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"webhook response was absent\")\n104: \t\t}\n105: \n106: \t\t// Response GVK and response.uid were not verified in v1beta1 handling, allow any\n107: \n108: \t\tpatch := []byte(nil)\n109: \t\tpatchType := admissionv1.PatchType(\"\")\n110: \t\tif mutating {\n111: \t\t\tpatch = r.Response.Patch\n112: \t\t\tif len(r.Response.Patch) > 0 {\n113: \t\t\t\t// patch type was fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected response type %T\", review)\n129: \t}\n130: }\n131: \n132: // CreateAdmissionObjects returns the unique request uid, the AdmissionReview object to send the webhook and to admission webhook chain is implemented across multiple Go packages that work together to handle dynamic admission control for API requests. The chain begins with the main Webhook handler in generic/webhook.go, which implements the core admission.Interface and orchestrates the entire webhook admission flow. When a request arrives, the Dispatch() method in generic/webhook.go coordinates with ShouldCallHook() to determine which webhooks should be invoked based on namespace selectors, object selectors, and resource rules. The actual webhook invocations are delegated to specialized Dispatcher implementations in the mutating and validating subpackages. For mutating webhooks, the mutatingDispatcher in mutating/dispatcher.go iterates through eligible webhooks and calls callAttrMutatingHook() for each one, which handles the HTTP request/response cycle, patch application, and reinvocation logic for consecutive mutations. The validatingDispatcher in validating/dispatcher.go runs validating webhooks in parallel (via goroutines) and aggregates their responses. Both dispatchers use the request/admissionreview.go utilities to create AdmissionReview objects via CreateAdmissionObjects() and validate responses via VerifyAdmissionResponse(). The WebhookAccessor interface (defined in accessors.go) provides a unified way to access webhook configuration details for both MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook types. The webhook configurations are managed by configuration managers (mutating_webhook_manager.go and validating_webhook_manager.go), which expose a generic.Source interface that provides lists of WebhookAccessor instances. The webhook matching logic leverages predicate matchers in the predicates subpackages (namespace/matcher.go, object/matcher.go, rules/rules.go) to determine if a webhook should be called based on the admission request attributes. Error handling is centralized in errors/statuserror.go which converts webhook rejections into appropriate status errors. The entire chain supports advanced features like reinvocation for mutating webhooks (via mutating/reinvocationcontext.go), parallel execution for validating webhooks, timeout handling, and detailed audit annotations for webhook invocations.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":864,"cache_read_input_tokens":93723,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":864},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"4060daf4-ff63-4ee2-91a9-644df5bce12c","uuid":"83009b58-9a61-4b4d-9abd-876e1db22926"}

admission webhook chain is implemented across multiple Go packages that work together to handle dynamic admission control for API requests. The chain begins with the main Webhook handler in generic/webhook.go, which implements the core admission.Interface and orchestrates the entire webhook admission flow. When a request arrives, the Dispatch() method in generic/webhook.go coordinates with ShouldCallHook() to determine which webhooks should be invoked based on namespace selectors, object selectors, and resource rules. The actual webhook invocations are delegated to specialized Dispatcher implementations in the mutating and validating subpackages. For mutating webhooks, the mutatingDispatcher in mutating/dispatcher.go iterates through eligible webhooks and calls callAttrMutatingHook() for each one, which handles the HTTP request/response cycle, patch application, and reinvocation logic for consecutive mutations. The validatingDispatcher in validating/dispatcher.go runs validating webhooks in parallel (via goroutines) and aggregates their responses. Both dispatchers use the request/admissionreview.go utilities to create AdmissionReview objects via CreateAdmissionObjects() and validate responses via VerifyAdmissionResponse(). The WebhookAccessor interface (defined in accessors.go) provides a unified way to access webhook configuration details for both MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook types. The webhook configurations are managed by configuration managers (mutating_webhook_manager.go and validating_webhook_manager.go), which expose a generic.Source interface that provides lists of WebhookAccessor instances. The webhook matching logic leverages predicate matchers in the predicates subpackages (namespace/matcher.go, object/matcher.go, rules/rules.go) to determine if a webhook should be called based on the admission request attributes. Error handling is centralized in errors/statuserror.go which converts webhook rejections into appropriate status errors. The entire chain supports advanced features like reinvocation for mutating webhooks (via mutating/reinvocationcontext.go), parallel execution for validating webhooks, timeout handling, and detailed audit annotations for webhook invocations.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
